	LOCAL_REFERENCE_CODE INTEGER NOT NULL,

	CLIENT_CATALOG_TYPE INTEGER,
	CLIENT_CATALOG_CODE VARCHAR(3),

	ACCESS_KEY VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
	TRANSACTION_DATE TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
	ZERO_FEE DECIMAL(12,2),
	IVA_FEE DECIMAL(12,2),
	TRANSACTION_VALUE DECIMAL(12,2) NOT NULL,
	REFERENCED_DOCUMENT_NUMBER VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
	NOTE_NUMBER VARCHAR(20),
	SISTAR_CONSUMPTION_VALUE DECIMAL(12,2),
	SISTAR_CONSUMPTION_DATE TIMESTAMP,
	SISTAR_CONSUMPTION_STATUS_TYPE INTEGER,
	SISTAR_CONSUMPTION_STATUS VARCHAR(3),
	CREDIT_VALUE_STATUS CHAR(1) DEFAULT '0' NOT NULL,
	OBSERVATIONS VARCHAR(1024),
	STATUS CHAR(1) DEFAULT '1' NOT NULL,
	CREATED_BY_USER VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
	CREATED_DATE TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
	LAST_MODIFIED_BY_USER VARCHAR(50),
	LAST_MODIFIED_DATE TIMESTAMP,
	"VERSION" INTEGER DEFAULT 1 NOT NULL,
	CREATED_FROM_IP VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
	UPDATED_FROM_IP VARCHAR(50),
	CONSTRAINT SSPSORPKCONCRENOT PRIMARY KEY (HEADER_ID)
);

CREATE INDEX SFSCTRFKCONCRENOTPKCATVALSTA ON SMXFINANC.SFSCTTCONCRENOT (SISTAR_CONSUMPTION_STATUS,SISTAR_CONSUMPTION_STATUS_TYPE);

	CODCATVALEVA DECIMAL(10,0),

	CODIGOCATALOGOASSESMENT INTEGER,

	CODCATVALPERFILKUDERT DECIMAL(10,0) DEFAULT NULL,

);

	CODIGOCOMPANIA INTEGER NOT NULL,
	SECUENCIALSERVIDOR INTEGER NOT NULL,
	DIRECCIONIP VARCHAR(256),
	PUERTO INTEGER,
	USUARIO VARCHAR(256),
	CLAVE VARCHAR(256),
	TIPSERCATTIP INTEGER,
	TIPSERCATVAL VARCHAR(3),
	SISTEMAOPERATIVO VARCHAR(32),
	ESTADO VARCHAR(3) NOT NULL,
	NOMBRESERVIDOR VARCHAR(256),
	DESCRIPCIONSERVIDOR VARCHAR(512),
	SEPARADORDIRECTORIO VARCHAR(8),
	USUARIOREGISTRO VARCHAR(32) NOT NULL,
	FECHAREGISTRO TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
	USUARIOMODIFICACION VARCHAR(32),
	FECHAMODIFICACION TIMESTAMP,
	PASSWORDENCRYPTED CHAR(1) DEFAULT NULL,
	RUTACLAVEPRIVADA VARCHAR(300)
);
